GrpcMuxImpl::onDiscoveryResponse(\\n314:     std::unique_ptr<envoy::service::discovery::v3::DiscoveryResponse>&& message,\\n315:     ControlPlaneStats& control_plane_stats) {\\n316:   const GrpcMuxImpl::processDiscoveryResources(const std::vector<DecodedResourcePtr>& resources,\\n414:                                             ApiState& api_state, const std::string& type_url,\\n415:                                             const std::string& version_info,\\n416:                                             const bool call_delegate) {\\n417:   ASSERT_IS_MAIN_OR_TEST_THREAD();\\n418: }\\n502:   }\\n503: \\n504:   // All config updates have been applied without throwing an exception, so we'll call the xDS\\n505:   // resources delegate, if any.\\n506:   if (call_delegate && GrpcMuxImpl::expiryCallback(absl::string_view type_url,\\n564:                                  const std::vector<std::string>& expired) {\\n565:   // The TtlManager triggers a callback with a list of   // To avoid O(n^2) explosion (e.g. when we have 1000s of EDS watches), we\\n419:   // build a map here from resource name to resource and then walk watches_.\\n420:   // We have to walk all watches
